śṛṇuyāt nityam mucyate sarva pātakaiḥ śrāvayet vā dvijān śāntān sa yāti paramām gatim iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca eṣā puṇyatamā devī deva gandharva sevitā narmadā loka vikhyātā tīrthānām uttamā nadī tasyāḥ śṛṇudhvam māhātmyam mārkaṇḍeyena bhāṣitam yudhiṣṭhirāya tu śubham sarva pāpa praṇāśanam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca śrutāḥ tu vividhāḥ dharmāḥ tvad prasādāt mahā mune māhātmyam ca prayāgasya tīrthāni vividhāni ca narmadā sarva tīrthānām mukhyā hi bhavatā īritā tasyāḥ tu idānīm māhātmyam vaktum arhasi sattama mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca narmadā saritām śreṣṭhā rudra dehāt viniḥ sṛtā tārayet sarva bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca narmadāyāḥ tu māhātmyam purāṇe yat mayā śrutam idānīm tat pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ śubham puṇyā kanakhale gaṅgā kurukṣetre sarasvatī grāme vā yadi vā araṇye puṇyā sarvatra narmadā tribhiḥ sārasvatam toyam sapta ahena tu yāmunam sadyas punāti gāṅgeyam darśanāt eva nārmadam kaliṅga deśa paśca ardhe parvate amarakaṇṭake puṇyā ca triṣu lokeṣu ramaṇīyā manoramā sa deva asura gandharvāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tapaḥ taptvā tu rāja indra siddhim tu paramām gatāḥ upoṣya rajanīm ekām kulānām tārayet śatam yojanānām śatam sāgram śrūyate sarit uttamā ṣaṣṭi tīrtha sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi koṭyaḥ tathā eva ca evam sarva samācāraḥ yaḥ tu prāṇān samutsṛjet tasya puṇya phalam rājan śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ nṛpa śata varṣa sahasrāṇi svarge modati pāṇḍava sapsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ divya strī parivāritaḥ tatas svargāt paribhraṣṭaḥ rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ālekhya vāhanaiḥ śubhraiḥ dāsī dāsa samanvitam jīvet varṣa śatam sāgram tatra bhoga samanvitaḥ paścime parvata taṭe sarva pāpa vināśanaḥ hradaḥ jaleśvaraḥ nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ tatra piṇḍa pradānena saṃdhyā upāsana karmaṇā daśa varṣāṇi pitaraḥ tarpitāḥ syuḥ na saṃśayaḥ dakṣiṇe narmadā kūle kapilā ākhyā mahā nadī sarala arjuna saṃcchannā na ati dūre vyavasthitā sā tu puṇyā mahābhāgā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā tatra koṭi śatam sāgram tīrthānām tu yudhiṣṭhira tasmin tīrthe tu ye vṛkṣāḥ patitāḥ kāla paryayāt narmadā toya saṃspṛṣṭāḥ te yānti paramām gatim dvitīyā tu mahābhāgā viśalyakaraṇī śubhā tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā viśalyaḥ bhavati kṣaṇāt kapilā ca viśalyā ca śrūyate rāja sattama īśvareṇa purā proktā lokānām hita kāmyayā anāśakam tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmin tīrthe narādhipa sarasvatyām ca gaṅgāyām narmadāyām yudhiṣṭhira samam snānam ca dānam ca yathā me śaṅkaraḥ abravīt varṣa koṭi śatam sāgram rudra loke mahīyate narmadāyām jalam puṇyam phena ūrmi samalaṅkṛtam narmadā sarvatas puṇyā brahma hatyā apahāriṇī jāleśvaram tīrtha varam sarva pāpa vināśanam aśvamedhāt daśaguṇam puṇyam āpnoti mānavaḥ nānā druma latā ākīrṇaḥ nānā puṣpa upaśobhitaḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ tathā ca indraḥ vidyādhara gaṇaiḥ saha pradakṣiṇam tu yaḥ kuryāt parvatam hi amarakaṇṭakam pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti kāverī nāma vipulā nadī iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge aṣṭātriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca narmadā saritām śreṣṭhā sarva pāpa vināśinī munibhiḥ kathitā pūrvam īśvareṇa svayaṃbhuvā munibhiḥ saṃstutā hi eṣā narmadā pravarā nadī rudra gātrāt viniṣkrāntāḥ lokānām hita kāmyayā nāmnā bhadreśvaram puṇyam sarva pāpa haram śubham tatas aṅgāreśvaram gacchet niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ tatra snātvā udakam kṛtvā sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt tatas puṣkariṇīm gacchet snānam tatra samācaret upoṣya rajanīm ekām snānam kṛtvā yathāvidhi ārādhayet mahā yogam devam nārāyaṇam harim ṛṣitīrtham tatas gatvā sarva pāpa haram nṛṇām yatra taptam tapaḥ pūrvam nāradena sura ṛṣiṇā brahmaṇā nirmitam liṅgam brahmeśvaram iti śrutam ṛṇatīrtham tatas gacchet saḥ ṛṇāt mucyate dhruvam yāvanti tasyāḥ romāṇi tad prasūti kuleṣu ca yaḥ tu prāṇa parityāgam kuryāt tatra narādhipa akṣayam modate kālam yāvat candra divākarau narmadā taṭam āśritya tiṣṭhante ye tu mānavāḥ te mṛtāḥ svargam āyānti santaḥ sukṛtinaḥ yathā nivartitā purā tatra vyāsa bhītā mahānadī huṅkāritā tu vyāsena dakṣiṇena tatas gatā pradakṣiṇam tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmin tīrthe yudhiṣṭhira trailokya viśrutam puṇyam tatra sannihitaḥ śivaḥ tatra stanātvā naraḥ rājan gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt ājanmanaḥ kṛtam pāpam snātaḥ tīvram vyapohati upāsate mahātmānam skandam śaktidhiram prabhum tatas gacchet āṅgirasam snānam tatra samācaret aṅgirāḥ yatra deveśam brahma putraḥ vṛṣadhvajam kuśatīrtham tatas gacchet sarva pāpa praṇāśanam koṭitīrtham tatas gacchet sarva pāpa praṇāśanam tatra strātvā naraḥ rājyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ narmadā dakṣiṇe kūle saṃgameśvaram uttamam ādityāyatanam ramyam īśvareṇa tu bhāṣitam tatra snātvā tu rāja indra dattvā dānam tu śaktitaḥ daridrāḥ vyādhitāḥ ye tu ye ca duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ tatra snātvā tu rāja indra śuciḥ bhūtvā prayatnataḥ caitra māse tu saṃprāpte śukla pakṣe trayodaśī ayodhyām tu samāsādya tīrtham śakrasya viśrutam yaḥ tu cāndrāyaṇam kuryāt tatra tīrthe samāhitaḥ agnipraveśam yaḥ kuryāt somatīrthe narādhipa jale ca anaśanam vā api na asau martyaḥ abhijāyate yodhanīpuram ākhyātam viṣṇoḥ sthānam anuttamam asurāḥ yodhitāḥ tatra vāsudevena koṭiśas tatra tīrtham samutpannam viṣṇu śrīkaḥ bhavet iha narmadā dakṣiṇe kūle tīrtham parama śobhanam tasmin tīrthe naraḥ snātvā upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyām śrdham kuryāt yathāvidhi tasmin tu dāpayet piṇḍān vaiśākhyān tu viśeṣataḥ snātvā samāhita manāḥ dambha mātsarya varjitaḥ tatra snātvā tu rāja indra viṣṇu loke mahīyate yatra nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ munonām bhāvitātmanām sva ātmānam darśayāmāsa liṅgam tat paramam padam snānam dānam ca tatra eva brāhmaṇānām ca bhojanam ca kṛtam pretya ananta phala pradam aṅkola mūle dadyāt ca piṇḍān ca eva yathāvidhi tāritāḥ pitaraḥ tena tṛpyanti ācandratārakam na asti tena tīrtham narmadāyām yudhiṣṭhira darśanāt sparśanāt tasya snāna dāna tapaḥ japāt śuklatīrtham iti khyātam sarva pāpa vināśanam pādapa agreṇa dṛṣṭena brahmahatyām vyapohati devyā saha sadā bhargaḥ tatra tiṣṭhati śaṅkaraḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśyām vaiśākhe māsi suvrata gaṇāḥ ca apsarasām nāgāḥ tatra tiṣṭhanti puṅgava rajakena yathā vastram śuklam bhavati vāriṇā ājanmani kṛtam pāpam śuklatīrthe vyapohati snānam dānam tapaḥ śrāddham anantam tatra dṛśyate śuklatīrthāt param tīrtham na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati pūrve vayasi karmāṇi kṛtvā pāpāni mānavaḥ kārtikasya tu māsasya kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśī tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yajña dānena vā punar na tām gatim avāpnoti śuklatīrthe tu yām labhet śuklatīrtham mahā tīrtham ṛṣi siddha niṣevitam ayane vā caturdaśyām saṃkrāntau viṣuve tathā snātvā tu sa upavāsaḥ san vijita ātmā samāhitaḥ dānam dadyāt yathāśakti prīyetām hari śaṅkarau anātham durgatam vipram nāthavantam atha api vā udvādayati yaḥ tīrthe tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśyām māgha māse yudhiṣṭhira snānam kṛtvā na paśyet yoni saṅkaṭam saṃgame tu naraḥ snāyāt upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ brāhmaṇam bhojayet ekam koṭiḥ bhavati bhojitāḥ eraṇḍīsaṃgame snātvā bhakti bhāvāt turañjitaḥ mṛttikām śirasi sthāpya avagāhya ca tat jalam tatas gaccheta rāja indra tīrtham kārṇāṭikeśvaram gaṅgā avatarate tatra dine puṇye na saṃśayaḥ jyeṣṭha māse tu saṃprāpte caturdaśyām viśeṣataḥ ghṛtena snāpayet rudram sa ghṛtam śrīphalam dahet ghaṇṭā ābharaṇa saṃyuktām kapilām vai pradāpayet sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktaḥ sarva deva namaskṛtaḥ śiva tulya balaḥ bhūtvā śiva vat krīḍate ciram aṅgārakadine prāpte caturthyām tu viśeṣataḥ snāpayitvā śivam dadyāt brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tu bhojanam sarva bhoga samāyuktaḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ aṅgāraka navamyām tu amāvāsyām tathā eva ca śrāvaṇe māsī saṃprāpte kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśī pitṝṇām tarpaṇam kṛtvā mucyate asau ṝṇa trayāt akāmaḥ vā sa kāmaḥ vā tatra snātvā tu mānavaḥ ājanma janitaiḥ pāpaiḥ mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tasya vai paścime deśe samīpe na ati dūratas daśāśvamedhikam tīrtham triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam upoṣya rajanīm ekām māsi bhādrapade śubhe amāvasyām naraḥ snātvā pūjayet vṛṣabhadhvajam kāñcanena vimānena kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinā pitṝṇām tarpaṇam kuryāt aśvamedha phalam labhet iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge ekonacatvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ uvāca tatra devaḥ bhṛguḥ rudram ārādhayat purā etat kṣetram su vipulam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam tatra snātvā divam yānti ye mṛtāḥ te apunarbhavāḥ upānahoḥ tathā yugmam deyam annam sa kāñcanam kṣaranti sarva dānāni yajña dānam tapaḥ kriyā akṣayam tat tapaḥ taptam bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira tasya eva tapasā ugreṇa tuṣṭena tripurāriṇā sānnidhyam tatra kathitam bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira yatra ārādhya triśūla aṅkam gautamaḥ siddhim āpnuyāt tatra snātvā naraḥ rājan upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ vṛṣotsargam tatas gacchet śāśvatam padam āpnuyāt na jānanti narāḥ mūḍhāḥ viṣṇoḥ māyā vimohitāḥ narmadāyām sthitam rājan sarva pātaka nāśanam tatra tīrthe tu rāja indra prāṇatyāgam karoti yaḥ vaset kalpa ayutam sāgram śiva tulya parākramaḥ kālena mahatā jātaḥ pṛthivyām ekarāj bhavet varāhatīrtham ākhyātam viṣṇu loka gati pradam paurṇamāsyām viśeṣeṇa snānam tatra samācaret śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyām snānam tatra samācaret yat tatra dīyate dānam sarvam koṭi guṇam bhavet sāvitrītīrtham āsādya yaḥ tu prāṇān parityajet asmin tīrthe mṛtaḥ rājan gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt aśvamedhāt daśaguṇam pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ etat tīrtham samāsādya yaḥ tu prāṇān parityajet jala praveśam yaḥ kuryāt tasmin tīrthe narādhipa eraṇḍyāḥ narmadāyāḥ tu saṃgamam loka viśrutam tatra tīrtham mahā puṇyam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam upavāsa paraḥ bhūtvā nityam vrata parāyaṇaḥ triguṇam ca aśvamedhasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ tatra upavāsam yaḥ kṛtvā paśyeta vimaleśvaram sapta janma kṛtam pāpam hitvā yāti śiva ālayam upoṣya rajanīm ekām niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ etāni tava saṃkṣepāt prādhānyāt kathitāni tu na śakyā vistarāt vaktum saṃkhyā tīrtheṣu pāṇḍava eṣā pavitrā vimalā nadī trailokya viśrutā narmadā saritām śreṣṭhā mahādevasya vallabhā cāndrāyaṇa śatam sāgram labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣāḥ nāstikyam ghoram āśritāḥ narmadām sevate nityam svayam devaḥ maheśvaraḥ tena puṇyā nadī jñeyā brahma hatyā apahāriṇī iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca mahādeva priya karam mahāpātaka nāśanam mahādevam didṛkṣūṇām ṛṣīṇaṇām parameṣṭhinām brahāmaṇā nirmitam sthānam tapaḥ taptum dvijottamāḥ marīcayaḥ atrayaḥ viprāḥ vasiṣṭhāḥ kratavaḥ tathā bhṛgavaḥ aṅgirasaḥ pūrvāḥ brahmāṇam kamalodbhavam ṣaṭkulīyāḥ ūcuḥ satram sahasram āsadhvam vāc manaḥ doṣa varjitāḥ deśam ca vaḥ pravakṣyāmi yasmin deśe cariṣyatha uktvā manaḥ mayam cakram sa sṛṣṭvā tān uvāca ha yatra asya nemiḥ śīryeta sa deśaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ naimisam tat smṛtam nāmnā puṇyam sarvatra pūjitam siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇam yakṣa gandharva sevitam atra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ imam deśam samāśritya ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ satreṇa ārādhya deveśam dṛṣṭavantaḥ maheśvaram atra dānam tapaḥ taptam snānam japya ādikam ca yat ekaikam pāvayet pāpam sapta janma kṛtam dvijāḥ atra pūrvam sa bhagavān ṛṣīṇām satram āsatām provāca vāyuḥ brahmāṇḍam purāṇam brahma bhāṣitam atra devaḥ mahādevaḥ rudrāṇyā kila viśvakṛt jajāpa rudram aniśam yatra nandī mahā gaṇaḥ dadau ātma samāna tvam mṛtyu vañcanam eva ca abhūt ṛṣiḥ sa dharma ātmā śilādaḥ nāma dharma vid ārādhayat mahādevam putra artham vṛṣabhadhvajam śarvaḥ sa umaḥ gaṇa vṛtaḥ vara daḥ asmi iti abhāṣata sa vavre varam īśānam vareṇyam girijāpatim ayoni jam mṛtyu hīnam dehi putram tvayā samam tatas yiyakṣuḥ svām bhūmim śilādaḥ dharma vittamaḥ cakarṣa lāṅgalena ūrvaḥ om bhittvā adṛśyata śobhanaḥ rūpa lāvaṇya saṃpannaḥ tejasā bhāsayan diśaḥ śilādam tāta tāta iti prāha nandī punar punar tam dṛṣṭvā nandanam jātam śilādaḥ pariṣasvaje munibhyaḥ darśayāmāsa ye tad āśrama vāsinaḥ jātakarma ādikāḥ sarvāḥ kriyāḥ tasya cakāra ha upanīya yathāśāstram vedam adhyāpayat sutam cakre maheśvaram draṣṭum jeṣye mṛtyum iti prabhum sa gatvā saritam puṇyām ekāgra śraddhayā anvitaḥ jajāpa rudram aniśam maheśa āsakta mānasaḥ tasya koṭyām tu pūrṇāyām śaṅkaraḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ āgatya sa ambaḥ sa gaṇaḥ vara daḥ asmi iti uvāca ha sa vavre punar eva aham japeyam koṭim īśvaram tāvat āyuḥ mahādeva dehi iti varam īśvara jajāpa koṭim bhagavān bhūyas tad gata mānasaḥ dvitīyāyām ca koṭyām vai saṃpūrṇāyām vṛṣadhvajaḥ āgatya vara daḥ asmi iti prāha bhūta gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ tṛtīyām japtum icchāmi koṭim bhūyas api śaṅkara koṭi traye atha saṃpūrṇe devaḥ prīta manāḥ bhṛśam āgatya vara daḥ asmi iti prāha bhūta gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ japeyam koṭim anyām vai bhūyas api tava tejasā mahāgaṇapatiḥ devyāḥ putraḥ bhava maheśvaraḥ yogi īśvaraḥ yoga netā gaṇānām īśvara īśvaraḥ sarva loka adhipaḥ śrīmān sarva jñaḥ mad bala anvitaḥ jñānam tat māmakam divyam hastāmalaka vat tava ā bhūta saṃplava sthāyī tatas yāsyasi mad padam etat uktvā mahādevaḥ gaṇān āhūya śaṅkaraḥ udvāhayāmāsa ca tam svayam eva pinākadhṛk marutām ca śubhām kanyām suyaśā iti ca viśrutām etat japya īśvaram sthānam devadevasya śūlinaḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca nāmnā pañcanadam puṇyam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam mahābhairavam iti uktam mahāpātaka nāśanam tīrthānām ca param tīrtham vitastā paramā nadī sarva pāpa harā puṇyā svayam eva girīndrajā tīrtham pañcatapam nāma śaṃbhoḥ amita tejasaḥ kāyāvarohaṇam nāma mahādeva ālayam śubham yatra māheśvarāḥ dharmāḥ munibhiḥ saṃpravartitāḥ śrāddham dānam tapaḥ homaḥ upavāsaḥ tathā akṣayaḥ tatra gatvā tyajet prāṇān lokān prāpnoti śāśvatān jāmadagnyasya tu śubham rāmasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ mahākālam iti khyātam tīrtham trailokya viśrutam gatvā prāṇān parityajya gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt tatra sannihitaḥ śrīmān bhagavān nakuli īśvaraḥ devyā saha mahādevaḥ nityam śiṣyaiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ tatra snātvā mahādevam pūjayitvā vṛṣadhvajam bhīmeśvaram iti khyātam gatvā muñcati pātakam tathā anyat caṇḍavegāyāḥ saṃbhedaḥ pāpa nāśanaḥ sarveṣām api ca eteṣām tīrthānām paramā purī nāmnā avārāṇasī divyā koṭi koṭi ayuta adhikā tasyāḥ purastāt māhātmyam bhāṣitam vaḥ mayā tu iha ete prādhānyataḥ proktāḥ deśāḥ pāpa harāḥ nṛṇām gatvā saṃkṣālayet pāpam janma antara śataiḥ kṛtam prāyaścittī ca vidhuraḥ tathā pāpa caraḥ gṛhī prakuryāt tīrtha saṃsevām ye ca anye tādṛśāḥ janāḥ ṛṇāni trīṇi apākṛtya kuryāt vā tīrtha sevanam vidhāya vṛttim putrāṇām bhāryām teṣu nidhāya ca prāyaścitta prasaṅgena tīrtha māhātmyam īritam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api mucyate sarva pātakaiḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca etat ākarṇya vijñānam nārāyaṇa mukha īritam munayaḥ ūcuḥ kathitāḥ bhavatā dharmāḥ mokṣa jñānam sa vistaram lokānām sarga vistāram vaṃśa manvantarāṇi ca bhūtānām bhūta bhavya īśa yathā pūrvam tvayā uditam sūtaḥ uvāca śrutvā teṣām tadā vākyam bhagavān kūrma rūpadhṛk vyājahāra mahā yogī bhūtānām pratisaṃcaram kūrmaḥ uvāca yaḥ ayam saṃdṛśyate nityam loke bhūta kṣayaḥ tu iha nityaḥ saṃkīrtyate nāmnā munibhiḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ mahāda ādyām viśeṣa antam yadā saṃyāti saṃkṣayam jñānāt ātyantikaḥ proktaḥ yoginaḥ parama ātmani naimittikam idānīm vaḥ kathayiṣye samāsatas sva ātma saṃsthāḥ prajāḥ kartum pratipede prajāpatiḥ tatas bhavati anāvṛṣṭiḥ tīvrā sā śata vārṣikī bhūta kṣaya karī ghorā sarva bhūta kṣayaṅkarī tatas yāni alpa sārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivī tale sapta raśmiḥ atho bhūtvā samuttiṣṭhan divākaraḥ tena āhāreṇa tāḥ dīptāḥ sūryāḥ sapta bhavanti uta tatas te raśmayaḥ sapta sūryāḥ bhūtvā caturdiśam vyāpnuvantaḥ ca te viprāḥ tu ūrdhvam ca adhas ca raśmibhiḥ dīpyante bhāskarāḥ sapta yuga anta agni pratāpinaḥ te sūryāḥ vāriṇā dīptāḥ bahu sāhastra raśmayaḥ kham samāvṛtya tiṣṭhanti nirdahantaḥ vasuṃdharām tatas teṣām pratāpena dahyamānā vasuṃdharā dīptābhiḥ saṃtatābhiḥ ca raśmibhiḥ vai samantataḥ sūrya agninā pramṛṣṭānām saṃsṛṣṭānām parasparam sarva loka praṇāśaḥ ca saḥ agniḥ bhūtvā su kuṇḍalī nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmiḥ kūrma pṛṣṭhā prakāśate ambarīṣam iva ābhāti sarvam āpūritam jagat dvīpān ca parvatān ca eva varṣāṇi atha mahā udadhīn tān sarvān bhasmasāt kṛtvā sapta ātmā pāvakaḥ prabhuḥ samudrebhyaḥ nadībhyaḥ ca pātālebhyaḥ ca sarvaśas tatas saṃvartakaḥ śailān atikramya mahān tathā lokān dahati dīpta ātmā rudra tejaḥ vijṝmbhitaḥ sa dagdhvā pṛthivīm devaḥ rasātalam aśoṣayat adhastāt pṛthivīm dagdhvā divam ūrdhvam dahiṣyati yojanānām śatāni iha sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca gandharvān ca piśācān ca sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasān dahet aśeṣam kālāgniḥ kālaḥ viśva tanuḥ svayam vyāpteṣu eteṣu lokeṣu tiryak ūrdhvam atha agninā tat tejaḥ samanuprāpya kṛtsnam jagat idam śanais ayaḥ guḍa nibham sarvam tadā ca ekam prakāśate tatas gaja kula unnādāḥ taḍidbhiḥ samalaṅkṛtāḥ uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakāḥ ghanāḥ kecid nīlotpala śyāmāḥ kecid kumuda sannibhāḥ dhūmra varṇāḥ tathā kecid kecid pītāḥ payodharāḥ kecid rāsabha varṇāḥ tu lākṣā rasa nibhāḥ tathā śaṅkha kunda nibhāḥ ca anye jāti añjana nibhāḥ pare manaḥ śilā ābhāḥ tu anye ca kapota sadṛśāḥ pare indracāpa nibhāḥ kecid uttiṣṭhanti ghanāḥ divi kecid parvata saṃkāśāḥ kecid gaja kula upamāḥ kūṭa aṅgāra nibhāḥ ca anye kecid mīna kula udvahāḥ bahūrūpāḥ ghorūpāḥ ghora svara ninādinaḥ tatas te jaladāḥ ghorāḥ rāviṇaḥ bhāskara ātmajāḥ saptadhā saṃvṛta ātmānaḥ tam agnim śamayanti uta su ghoram aśivam sarvam nāśayanti ca pāvakam naṣṭe ca agnau varṣa śataiḥ payodāḥ kṣaya saṃbhavāḥ dhārābhiḥ pūrayanti idam codyamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvā sa adri dvīpā tathā pṛthvī jalaiḥ saṃcchādyate śanais āditya raśmibhiḥ pītam jalam abhreṣu tiṣṭhati punar patati tat bhūmau pūryante tena ca arṇavāḥ tatas samudrāḥ svām velām atikrāntāḥ tu kṛtsnaśas tasmin ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame yoganindrām samāsthāya śete devaḥ prajāpatiḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ tathā kalpāḥ brahma viṣṇu śiva ātmakāḥ kathitāḥ hi purāṇeṣu munibhiḥ kāla cintakaiḥ sāttvikeṣu atha kalpeṣu māhātmyam adhikam hareḥ tāmaseṣu harasya uktam rājaseṣu prajāpateḥ yaḥ ayam pravartate kalpaḥ vārāhaḥ sāttvikaḥ mataḥ anye ca sāttvikāḥ kalpāḥ mama teṣu parigrahaḥ dhyānam tapaḥ tathā jñānam labdhvā teṣu eva yoginaḥ ārādhya giriśam mām ca yānti tat paramam padam saḥ aham sattvam samāsthāya māyī māyā mayīm svayam mām paśyanti mahātmānaḥ suptam kālam mahā ṛṣayaḥ jana loke vartamānāḥ tapasā yoga cakṣuṣā aham purāṇapuruṣaḥ bhūrbhuvaḥ prabhavaḥ vibhuḥ mantraḥ agniḥ brāhmiṇāḥ gāvaḥ kuśāḥ ca samidhaḥ hi aham prokṣaṇī ca śruvaḥ ca eva somaḥ ghṛtam atha asmi aham saṃvartakaḥ mahān ātmā pavitram paramam yaśaḥ haṃsaḥ prāṇaḥ atha kapilaḥ viśvamūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtiḥ kālaḥ jagat bījam atha amṛtam nārāyaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ yoga mūrtiḥ mām paśyanti yatayaḥ yoga niṣṭhā jñātvā ātmānam amṛta tvam vrajanti iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge tricatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kūrmaḥ uvāca prākṛtam hi samāsena śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama sva ātmani ātmānam āveśya bhūtvā devaḥ maheśvaraḥ dahet aśeṣam brahmāṇḍam sa deva asura mānuṣam tam āviśya mahādevaḥ bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ karoti loka saṃhāram bhīṣaṇam rūpam āśritaḥ praviśya maṇḍalam sauram kṛtvā asau bahudhā punar devatānām śarīreṣu kṣipati akhila dāhakam dagdheṣu aśeṣa deveṣu devī giri vara ātmajā ekāsā sākṣiṇī śaṃbhoḥ tiṣṭhate vaidikī śrutiḥ śiraḥ kapālaiḥ devānām kṛta straj vara bhūṣaṇaḥ āditya candra ādi gaṇaiḥ pūrayan vyoma maṇḍalam daṃṣṭrā karāla vadanaḥ pradīpta anala locanaḥ triśūlī kṛtti vasanaḥ yogam aiśvaram āsthitaḥ pītvā tat parama ānandam prabhūtam amṛtam svayam karoti tāṇḍavam devīm ālokya parameśvaraḥ pītvā nṛtta amṛtam devī bhartuḥ parama maṅgalā yogam āsthāya devasya deham āyāti śūlinaḥ saṃtyaktvā tāṇḍava rasam sva icchayā eva pinākadhṛk jyotiḥ svabhāvam bhagavān dagdhvā brahmāṇḍa maṇḍalam saṃsthiteṣu atha deveṣu brahma viṣṇu pinākiṣu guṇaiḥ aśeṣaiḥ pṛthivī vilayam yāti vāriṣu sa vāri tattvam sa guṇam grasate havyavāhanaḥ tejaḥ tu guṇa saṃyuktam vāyau saṃyāti saṃkṣayam ākāśe sa guṇaḥ vāyuḥ pralayam yāti viśva bhṛt bhūtādau ca tathā ākāśam līyate guṇa saṃyutam indriyāṇi ca sarvāṇi taijase yānti saṃkṣayam vaikārike deva gaṇāḥ pralaṃya yānti sattamāḥ vaikārikaḥ taijasaḥ ca bhūtādiḥ ca iti sattamāḥ evam saṃhṛtya bhūtāni tattvāni ca maheśvaraḥ viyojayati ca anyonyam pradhānam puruṣam param pradhāna puṃsoḥ ajayoḥ eṣa saṃhāraḥ īritaḥ guṇa sāmyam tat avyaktam prakṛtiḥ parigīyate kūṭasthaḥ cit mayaḥ hi ātmā kevalaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ gīyate munibhiḥ sākṣī mahān ekaḥ pitāmahaḥ evam saṃhāra karaṇī śaktiḥ māheśvarī dhruvā pradhāna ādyam viśeṣa antam dahet rudraḥ iti śrutiḥ yoginām atha sarveṣām jñāna vinyasta cetasām ātyantikam ca eva layam vidadhāti iha śaṅkaraḥ iti eṣa bhagavān rudraḥ saṃhāram kurute vaśī sthāpikā mohanī śaktiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutiḥ sṛjet aśeṣam prakṛteḥ tad mayaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ sarva jñāḥ sarva gāḥ śāntāḥ sva ātmani eva vyavasthitāḥ śaktayaḥ brahma viṇu īśāḥ bhukti mukti phala pradāḥ sarva īśvarāḥ sarva vandyāḥ śāśvata ananta bhoginaḥ ekam eva akṣaram tattvam pum pradhāna īśvara ātmakam anyāḥ ca śaktayaḥ divyāḥ santi tatra sahasraśas ijyante vividhaiḥ yajñaiḥ śakra āditya ādayaḥ amarāḥ ekaikasya sahasrāṇi dehānām vai śatāni ca tām tām śaktim samādhāya svayam devaḥ maheśvaraḥ ijyate sarva yajñeṣu brāhmaṇaiḥ veda vādibhiḥ sarva kāma pradaḥ rudraḥ iti eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ sarvāsām eva śaktīnām brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ prādhānyena smṛtāḥ devāḥ śaktayaḥ paramātmanaḥ ādyaḥ parastāt bhagavān parama ātmā sanātanaḥ gīyate sarva śakti ātmā śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ brahma viṣṇau agni varuṇāḥ sarve devāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ tat tat rūpam samāsthāya pradadāti phalam śivaḥ tasmāt ekataram bhedam samāśritya api śāśvatam ārādhayat mahādevam yāti tat paramam padam kintu devam mahādevam sarva śaktim sanātanam ārādhayet vai giriśam sa guṇam vā atha nirguṇam mayā proktaḥ hi bhavatām yogaḥ prāk eva nirguṇaḥ ārurukṣuḥ tu sa guṇam pūjayet parameśvaram pinākinam trinayanam jaṭilam kṛttivāsasam padmāsana stham rukma ābham cintayet vaidikī śrutiḥ eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sa bījaḥ muni sattamāḥ ārādhayet virūpākṣam ādi madhya anta saṃsthitam tādṛśam rūpam āsthāya samāyā ātyantikam śivam eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sabījaḥ atyanta bhāvane yathāvidhi prakurvāṇaḥ prāpnuyāt aiśvaram padam atra api aśaktaḥ atha haram viṣṇum bahmāṇam arcayet atha ced asamarthaḥ syāt tatra api muni puṅgavāḥ tatas vāyu agni śakra ādīn pūjayet bhakti saṃyutaḥ jñānam tat uktam nirbojam pūrvam hi bhavatām mayā viṣṇum rudram virañcim ca sa bījam bhāvayet budhaḥ devān tatparaḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ pūjayet puruṣam viṣṇum catur mūrti dharam harim an ādi nidhanam devam vāsudevam sanātanam nārāyaṇam jagadyonim ākāśam paramam padam tad liṅga dhārī niyatam tad bhaktaḥ tad apāśrayaḥ iti etat kathitam jñānam bhāvanā saṃśrayam param sūtaḥ uvāca etāvat uktvā bhagavān virarāma janārdanaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ munayaḥ viṣṇum śakreṇa saha mādhavam munayaḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ te kūrma rūpāya viṣṇave paramātmane nārāyaṇāya viśvāya vāsudevāya te namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ te kṛṣṇāya govindāya namaḥ namaḥ mādhavāya namaḥ tubhyam namaḥ yajñeśvarāya ca sahasra śirase tubhyam sahasra akṣāya te namaḥ om namaḥ jñāna rūpāya paramātma svarūpiṇe ānandāya namaḥ tubhyam māyā atītāya te namaḥ namaḥ gūḍha śarīrāya nirguṇāya namaḥ astu te puruṣāya purāṇāya sattā mātra svarūpiṇe namaḥ sāṃkhyāya yogāya kevalāya namaḥ astu te dharma jñāna adhigamyāya niṣkalāya namaḥ namaḥ parāvarāṇām prabhave veda vedyāya te namaḥ namaḥ astu te varāhāya nārasiṃhāya te namaḥ vāmanāya namaḥ tubhyam hṛṣīkeśāya te namaḥ namaḥ astu kālarudrāya kāla rūpāya te namaḥ devānām pataye tubhyam deva ārti śamanāya te asmābhiḥ viditam jñānam yat jñātvā amṛtam aśnute śrutāḥ tu vividhāḥ dharmāḥ vaṃśāḥ manvantarāṇi ca tvam hi sarva jagat sākṣī viśvaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ trātum arhasi ananta ātman tvam eva śaraṇam gatiḥ sūtaḥ uvāca kaurmam purāṇam akhilam yat jagāda gadādharaḥ asmin purāṇe lakṣmyāḥ tu saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ purā mohāya aśeṣa bhūtānām vāsudevena yojanam prajāpatīnām sargaḥ tu varṇa dharmāḥ ca vṛttayaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām yathāvat lakṣaṇam śubham pitāmahasya viṣṇoḥ ca maheśasya ca dhīmataḥ ekatvam ca pṛthaktvam ca viśeṣaḥ ca upavarṇitaḥ bhaktānām lakṣaṇam proktam samācāraḥ ca śobhanaḥ varṇa āśramāṇām kathitam yathāvat iha lakṣaṇam ādisargaḥ tatas paścāt aṇḍa āvaraṇa saptakam hiraṇyagarbha sargaḥ ca kīrtitaḥ muni puṅgavāḥ kāla saṃkhyā prakathanam māhātmyam ca īśvarasya ca brahmaṇaḥ śayanam ca apsu nāma nirvacanam tathā varāha vapuṣā bhūyas bhūmeḥ uddharaṇam punar vyākhyataḥ rudra sargaḥ ca ṛṣi sargaḥ ca tāpasaḥ darśanam ca maheśasya māhātmyam viṣṇunā īritam divya dṛṣṭi pradānam ca brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ saṃstavaḥ devadevasya brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā saṃvādaḥ viṣṇunā sārdham śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ vara dānam tathāpūrvam antardhānam pinākinaḥ ekībhāvaḥ ca devasya viṣṇunā kathitaḥ tatas vimohaḥ brahmaṇaḥ ca atha saṃjñā lābhaḥ hareḥ tatas tapaḥ caraṇam ākhyātam devadevasya dhīmataḥ prādurbhāvaḥ maheśasya lalāṭāt kathitaḥ tatas rudrāṇām kathitā sṛṣṭiḥ brahmaṇaḥ pratiṣedhanam darśanam devadevasya nara nārī śarīra tā devyāḥ vibhāga kathanam devadevāt pinākinaḥ nāmnām sahasram kathitam pitrā himavatā svayam bhṛgu ādīnām prajā sargaḥ rājñām vaṃśasya vistaraḥ tatas ca śāpaḥ kathitaḥ munīnām muni puṅgavāḥ rudra āgatiḥ prasādaḥ ca antardhānam pinākinaḥ pitāmahasya upadeśaḥ kīrtyate rakṣaṇāya tu hiraṇyakaśipoḥ nāśaḥ hiraṇyākṣa vadhaḥ tathā tatas ca śāpaḥ kathitaḥ devadāru vanaukasām prahrāda nigrahaḥ ca atha baleḥ saṃyamanam tatas bāṇasya nigrahaḥ ca atha prasādaḥ tasya śūlinaḥ ṛṣīṇām vaṃśa vistāraḥ rājñām vaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ vara lābhaḥ mahādevam dṛṣṭvā sa ambam trilocanam kailāsa gamanam ca atha nivāsaḥ tatra śārṅgiṇaḥ tatas ca kathyate bhītiḥ dvārivatyāḥ nivāsinām rakṣaṇam garuḍena atha jitvā śatrūn mahā balān nārāt āgamanam ca eva yātrā ca eva garutmataḥ tatas ca kṛṣṇa āgamanam munīnām āgatiḥ tatas naityakam vāsudevasya śiva liṅga arcanam tathā mārkaṇḍeyasya ca muneḥ praśnaḥ proktaḥ tatas param liṅga arcana nimittam ca liṅgasya api sa liṅginaḥ yathātmya kathanam ca atha liṅga āvirbhāvaḥ eva ca brahma viṣṇoḥ tathā madhye kīrtitaḥ muni puṅgavāḥ saṃstavaḥ devadevasya prasādaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ kṛṣṇasya gamane buddhiḥ ṛṣīṇām āgatiḥ tathā anuvaśāsitam ca kṛṣṇena vara dānam mahātmanaḥ gamanam ca eva kṛṣṇasya pārthasya api ca darśanam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya uktāḥ yuga dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ anugrahaḥ atha pārthasya vārāṇasī gatiḥ tatas pārāśaryasya ca muneḥ vyāsasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ vāraṇasyāḥ ca māhātmyam tīrthānām ca eva varṇanam tīrtha yātrā ca vyāsasya devyāḥ ca eva atha darśanam prayāgasya ca māhātmyam kṣetrāṇām atha kīrtinam phalam ca vipulam viprāḥ mārkaṇḍeyasya nirgamaḥ bhuvanānām sva rūpam ca jyotiṣām ca niveśanam kīrtyante ca eva varṣāṇi nadīnām ca eva nirṇayaḥ parvatānām ca kathanam sthānāni ca divaukasām dvīpānām pravibhāgaḥ ca śvetadvīpa upavarṇanam śayanam keśavasya atha māhātmyam ca mahātmanaḥ manvantarāṇām kathanam viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam eva ca veda śākhā praṇayanam vyāsānām kathanam tatas a vedasya ca vedānām kathanam muni puṅgavāḥ yoga īśvarāṇām ca kathā śiṣyāṇām ca atha kīrtanam gītāḥ ca vividha aguhyāḥ īśvarasya atha kīrtitāḥ varṇa āśramāṇām ācārāḥ prāyaścitta vidhiḥ tatas pativratāyāḥ ca ākhyānam tīrthānām ca vinirṇayaḥ tathā maṅkaṇakasya atha nigrahaḥ kīrtyate dvijāḥ vadhaḥ ca kathitaḥ viprāḥ kālasya ca samāsatas devadāru vane śaṃbhoḥ praveśaḥ mādhavasya ca darśanam ṣaṭkulīyānām devadevasya dhīmataḥ prākṛtaḥ pralayaḥ ca ūrdhvam sa bījaḥ yogaḥ eva ca evam jñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepam kīrtayet tu yaḥ evam uktvā śriyam devīm ādāya puruṣottamaḥ saṃtyajya kūrma saṃsthānam sva sthānam ca jagāma ha devāḥ ca sarve munayaḥ svāni sthānāni bhejire praṇamya puruṣam viṣṇum gṛhītvā hi amṛtam dvijāḥ etat purāṇam paramam bhāṣitam kūrma rūpiṇā sākṣāt deva ādidenena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā tatas svargāt paribhraṣṭaḥ viprāṇām jāyate kule pūrva saṃskāra māhātmyāt brahma vidyām avāpnuyāt śrotavyam ca dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ mahāpātaka nāśanam ekatas tu purāṇāni sa itihāsāni kṛtsnaśas dharma naipuṇya kāmānām jñāna naipuṇya kāminām idam purāṇam muktvā ekam na asti anyat sādhanam param yathāvat atra bhagavān devaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ hariḥ kathyate hi yathā viṣṇuḥ na tathā anyeṣu suvratāḥ brāhmī paurāṇikī ca iyam saṃhitā pāpa nāśanī tīrthānām paramam tīrtham tapasām ca param tapaḥ jñānānām paramam jñānam vratānām paramam vratam na adhyetavyam idam śāstram vṛṣalasya ca sannidhau yaḥ adhīte sa tu moha ātmā sa yāti narakān bahūn śrāddhe vā daivike kārye śrāvaṇīyam dvijātibhiḥ yajña ante tu viśeṣeṇa sarva doṣa viśodhanam mumukṣūṇām idam śāstram adhyetavyam viśeṣataḥ śrotavyam ca atha mantavyam veda artha paribṛṃhaṇam jñātvā yathāvat vipra indrān śrāvayet bhakti saṃyutān yaḥ aśraddadhāne puruṣe dadyāt ca adhārmike tathā sa pretya gatvā nirayān śunām yonim vrajati adhas namaskṛtvā harim viṣṇum jagadyonim sanātanam adhyetavyam idam śāstram kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam tathā iti ājñā devadevasya viṣṇoḥ amita tejasaḥ pārāśaryasya viprarṣeḥ vyāsasya ca mahātmanaḥ śrutvā nārāyaṇāt divyām nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ gautamāya dadau pūrvam tasmāt ca eva parāśaraḥ parāśaraḥ api gaṅgādvāre muni īśvarāḥ brahmaṇā kathitam pūrvam sanakāya ca dhīmate sanatkumārāya tathā sarva pāpa praṇāśanam sanakāt bhagavān sākṣāt devalaḥ yoga vittamaḥ sanatkumārāt bhagavān muniḥ satyavatī sutaḥ lebhe purāṇam paramam vyāsaḥ sarva artha saṃcayam tasmāt vyāsāt aham śrutvā bhavatām pāpa nāśanam pārāśaryāya śāntāya namaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmane namaḥ tasmai sureśāya viṣṇave kūrma rūpiṇe iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām upari vibhāge catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ upari vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇam samāptam
